# Graph Report - headroom  (2026-07-13)

## Corpus Check
- 1714 files · ~2,821,559 words
- Verdict: corpus is large enough that graph structure adds value.

## Summary
- 38305 nodes · 76835 edges · 1171 communities (1049 shown, 122 thin omitted)
- Extraction: 92% EXTRACTED · 8% INFERRED · 0% AMBIGUOUS · INFERRED: 5936 edges (avg confidence: 0.58)
- Token cost: 0 input · 0 output

## Graph Freshness
- Built from commit: `20ba068b`
- Run `git rev-parse HEAD` and compare to check if the graph is stale.
- Run `graphify update .` after code changes (no API cost).
